OrgUser Role Assignment\\nThe core role assignment at the organization level is managed by `pkg/services/org/`. The `OrgUser` struct in `pkg/services/org/model.go` (line 38) represents the assignment of a user to an organization with a specific role (RoleType: Admin, Editor, Viewer, or None). The role lifecycle is managed through `AddOrgUserCommand`, `UpdateOrgUserCommand`, and `RemoveOrgUserCommand`. These commands are implemented in `pkg/services/org/orgimpl/org.go` where `AddOrgUser()` (line 175), `UpdateOrgUser()` (line 180), and `RemoveOrgUser()` (line 185) delegate to the SQL store at `pkg/services/org/orgimpl/store.go`. HTTP endpoints are exposed through `pkg/api/org_users.go` and `pkg/api/org.go`.\\n\\n## 2. Team Group Sync\\nTeam management is centralized in `pkg/services/team/`. The `Team` model (in `pkg/services/team/model.go` line 24) includes an `ExternalUID` field (line 30) for external group mapping. Team members are represented by the `TeamMember` struct (line 132), with an `External` flag (line 138) indicating LDAP/OAuth-synced membership. The `AddOrUpdateTeamMemberHook()` and `RemoveTeamMemberHook()` functions in `pkg/services/team/teamimpl/store.go` (lines 405, 457) handle team membership modifications.\\n\\nExternal group sync occurs through multiple paths:\\n- LDAP: `pkg/services/ldap/ldap_groups.go` defines the `Groups` interface for team synchronization\\n- Authn sync layer: `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/sync/user_sync.go` contains the `UserSync` type that orchestrates team syncing via `syncTeams()` function\\n- OAuth connectors: `pkg/login/social/connectors/github_oauth.go`, `generic_oauth.go`, and `azuread_oauth.go` extract groups from identity providers\\n- The authn pipeline sets the `SyncTeams` flag in `pkg/services/authn/authn.go` (line 55) to enable team synchronization\\n\\n## 3.
